    8-bit bytestrings (like text_factory = str). It is highly
    recommended that you instead just switch your application
    to Unicode strings. [SQL: u'SELECT statement.id AS statement_id,
    statement.text AS statement_text, statement.extra_data AS
    statement_extra_data \nFROM statement \nWHERE statement.text
    = ?\n LIMIT ? OFFSET ?']
    [parameters: ('\xe4\xbd\xa0\xe5\xa5\xbd\xe5\x90\x97', 1, 0)]

    Revert "Move relational fields out of abstract base models"

34	23	chatterbot/ext/django_chatterbot/models.py

commit e13a69d98dab17fbc7fee178fb51b2af2faf40a0
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-10-03 07:06:52 -0400

    Move relational fields out of abstract base models
    
    ChatterBot's abstract base models for Django are suppose to make
    it easier for a developer to create a new model, based on the
    existing ones with their own modifications.
    
    Unfortunately, having related fields like foregin keys will result
    in errors when trying to create new models because the fields of
    the abstract parent class are still evaluated by Django and
    because they can only reference the origional models.

23	34	chatterbot/ext/django_chatterbot/models.py

commit 3c987a4f26435e61c92e312bf9cc009676983074
Author: Andrew C Bates <a@sprock.io>
Date:   2017-01-13 22:58:36 -0800

    Fix "empty generator" bug in ChatBot.filters
    
    This fixes a bug with the assignment of the filters attribute, whereby a
    generator, rather than it's result is assigned to the ChatBot.filters
    attribute. Subsequent iterations of the attribute will return an empty
    result.
    
    This fix just assigns the result to the filters attribute as a tuple.

commit d81039f9913278852bb57c1b0bf89551aa095cc9
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2017-01-03 08:13:24 -0500

    Disconnect storage from adapter class
    
    This makes a change to seperate the storage adapter from the base
    Adapter class. This is being done because the methods on the base
    Adapter class are not needed on the storage adapter.
    
    The main change is that is no longer possible for the storage
    adapter to access the ChatBot instance. This should not cause
    any probems because there are no "known" use cases where this
    is needed.
    
    This also allows a special case to be removed in the class
    validation utility so that a check to the "Adapter" class
    is never made. This allows the class validation utility to
    be more generic.

0	1	chatterbot/chatterbot.py
32	12	chatterbot/storage/storage_adapter.py
0	8	chatterbot/utils.py

commit 130670b6ce8df88ce37f8e1de502559fdd00a3c4
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-11-28 15:25:26 -0500

    Prevent possible edge case when adding inserting logic adapters
    
    The MultiLogicAdapter which handles the process of checking the
    generated responses of other logic adapters, could return just
    the user's input if other logic adapters are added after the
    chat bot is initialized. This was fixed by adding a separate
    list for system logic adapters that are required to be present
    at all times.

commit a644c4b125b51eec9380dce73956943a59e29137
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-11-27 20:55:07 -0500

    Update scope of external package imports
    
    In some cases, having these packages imported on the global level
    caused errors durring the installation process. This is because
    some ChatterBot classes are imported in __init__.py files and
    the main __init__.py in the chatterbot modue is imported by
    setup.py. As a result, the external packages are imported before
    they get installed.

commit 8856bce1fad2ae387e4bfc5eccd7ac256f4b0081
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-05-12 18:57:06 -0400

    Removed weather logic adapter.
    
    The weather logic adapter has a new home:
    https://github.com/gunthercox/chatterbot-weather
    
    It was removed from the main chatterbot project
    to keep the number of requirements low. On top
    of that, the weather logic adapter was also
    completely untested, undocumented, and contained
    multiple TODOs. In order to keep the quality of
    chatterbot's software as high as possible this
    adapter had to be pruned.
    
    In the future it will be possible to download
    the new chatterbot-weather module from PyPi.

0	1	chatterbot/adapters/logic/__init__.py
0	69	chatterbot/adapters/logic/weather.py
0	1	requirements.txt

commit e2055a272607d7efac4210fcb3993dcec64deb26
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-05-09 10:21:00 -0400

    Changed input/output parameter requirements.
    
    ChatterBot now requires a list of input and output adapter pairs
    to be provided. Any number of pairs can be added, and each pair
    must be a tuple containing only two elements. The first element
    must be the dot notated import path to an input adapter and the
    second element must be the dot notated import path to an output
    adapter.

    as a whole.

commit e5a986968a0844549283d14ae77d60a98d2987a1
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-05-08 09:17:54 -0400

    Increased efficiency of update method
    
    This makes changes to use the upsert attribute in mongodb so that
    documents are only created if they do not already exist.
    
    This change removes the need to call the find method to check if
    a statement already exists in the database. This reduces the
    number of database transactions that are required to complete
    the operation.

commit b0be0cc70837eb747b717b867705f08d6a1b25f0
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2016-02-11 07:38:56 -0500

    Remove Adaptation base object.
    
    This removes the Adaptation object from which the main ChatBot
    class was inheriting. Adaptation was intended to keep some of
    the implementation details out of the main class to keep the
    code clean and readable. However this did not work as intended.
    
    Due to the number of emails I have received asking questions
    about it, I have decided to move it back to the man ChatBot
    class so that all of the initialization for the ChatBot happens
    in one place.

commit 46ac754698910a4172e8caef094dffde614d4223
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-12-25 17:45:56 -0500

    Each adapter can now reference other adapter types.
    
    This addition makes changes so that adapters can take other adapters
    as a parameter. The reason for this change is because it is needed
    for logic adapters. Logic adapters should be able to access the
    storage adapter to retrieve information. It is more efficient to
    allow logic adapters direct access to the database than it is to
    pass in a list of known statements as is currently done. With this
    in mind, I have given all adapters access to each other to keep
    the interfaces unified and easy to work with.

commit 87c869e509f051fc4f0e3b3614dfa7ead3f8cc60
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-11-27 21:55:38 -0500

    Logic adapters should raise an exception if a list of options in not provided.
    
    This adds a new exception class to be used in these cases.
    The reason for making this change is because previously,
    logic adapters returned the input statement in the case that
    the list of possible options is empty. This gives a false
    positive that an exact match to the statement exists in the
    list. Instead, an exception should be thrown.

    Previously, if tests failed, randomly named test databases could
    be left behind. This change makes it so that all test data files
    are created within a directory which is created and removed after
    tests have finished. In the case on an exception, a directory is
    easier to manually clean up than many data files.

commit 5c4db23be1fd09348d2f26167462c6ade7076500
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-08-22 21:28:13 -0400

    Added Signature object.
    
    A signature object has been added. In the future, a statement may
    have multiple signatures. Each signature will contain the name of
    the user who said it, the date on which it was said, and any other
    useful meta-data which may be required.
    
    For now, statement objects still maintain the legacy name and date
    fields. These two attributes will be removed in the future in favor
    of the signature object.

commit 4b3acb1e12abe4b906826cbaab7bc8ccdacc283d
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-06-06 12:53:34 -0400

    Logic adapter now takes two parameters.
    
    The logic adapter now takes two parameters.
    The first is a statement string. The second is a list of strings
    that may contain possible matches.
    
    This change simplifies testing and makes it easier to write logic
    adapters. This change also prevents other adapters from being
    needing to be passed to each other.

commit 8afea1f79ad0e8e0aca20fed13d14663baa05865
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-06-06 07:10:09 -0400

    Created database controller layer.
    
    This change was made to allow the future creation of additional
    database adapters. This change starts to make alterations that
    will make it easier to connect different database types. The
    future goal will be to have data move as specified in the
    following outline:
    
    Layer 1: ChatterBot
      - This layer interacts with users and apis. It handles a simple
    api that allow responce data to be entered.
    
    Layer 2: Storage Controller
      - This layer recieves raw text or json data from layer 1.
      - Here, raw data is converted into Statement objects.
      - Statement objects can be modified and passed to Layer 3.
      - Statement objects can also be retreived from Layer 3.
    
    Layer 3: Database Adapter
      - The database adapter layer is an implementation of a
    simple interface that specifies basic operations that are
    required to use a type of database. These methods include
    getting and writing data.

commit 1c936fcd0526d21f60afb5d150937cb0c6572471
Author: Gunther Cox <gunthercx@gmail.com>
Date:   2015-01-31 20:29:12 -0500

    Chatterbot now stores information in a dictionary.
    
    This change fixes a major issue with how the chatterbot functions.
    Previously the chatterbot recorded the entire conversation including
    its own responces. As a result it was corrupting its own output.
    
    The chatterbot now stores only the responces entered by the user.
